<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of submachine guns</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><p>This is a <b>list of submachine guns</b>. It includes <a href="/wiki/Assault_rifle" title="Assault rifle">assault rifles</a> chambered for submachine gun or pistol cartridges, some <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Machine_pistols" title="Machine pistols">machine pistols</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Personal_defense_weapon" title="Personal defense weapon">personal defense weapons</a> (PDWs), all of which are sometimes designated as submachine guns.</p>
<p>Below is the list of <a href="/wiki/Submachine_gun" title="Submachine gun">submachine guns</a>. The table is sortable for every column.</p>
